\documentclass[frontgrid, backgrid]{flacards}\usepackage[]{graphicx}\usepackage[]{xcolor}
% maxwidth is the original width if it is less than linewidth
% otherwise use linewidth (to make sure the graphics do not exceed the margin)
\makeatletter
\def\maxwidth{ %
  \ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth
    \linewidth
  \else
    \Gin@nat@width
  \fi
}
\makeatother

\definecolor{fgcolor}{rgb}{0.345, 0.345, 0.345}
\newcommand{\hlnum}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.686,0.059,0.569}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstr}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.192,0.494,0.8}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlcom}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.678,0.584,0.686}{\textit{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlopt}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0,0,0}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.345,0.345,0.345}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwa}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.161,0.373,0.58}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwb}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.69,0.353,0.396}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwc}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.333,0.667,0.333}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.737,0.353,0.396}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\let\hlipl\hlkwb

\usepackage{framed}
\makeatletter
\newenvironment{kframe}{%
 \def\at@end@of@kframe{}%
 \ifinner\ifhmode%
  \def\at@end@of@kframe{\end{minipage}}%
  \begin{minipage}{\columnwidth}%
 \fi\fi%
 \def\FrameCommand##1{\hskip\@totalleftmargin \hskip-\fboxsep
 \colorbox{shadecolor}{##1}\hskip-\fboxsep
     % There is no \\@totalrightmargin, so:
     \hskip-\linewidth \hskip-\@totalleftmargin \hskip\columnwidth}%
 \MakeFramed {\advance\hsize-\width
   \@totalleftmargin\z@ \linewidth\hsize
   \@setminipage}}%
 {\par\unskip\endMakeFramed%
 \at@end@of@kframe}
\makeatother

\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{.97, .97, .97}
\definecolor{messagecolor}{rgb}{0, 0, 0}
\definecolor{warningcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 1}
\definecolor{errorcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 0}
\newenvironment{knitrout}{}{} % an empty environment to be redefined in TeX

\usepackage{alltt}

\usepackage{xcolor}
\usepackage{graphicx, tikz}



\newlength{\cardwidthspace}
\newlength{\cardheightspace}
\newlength{\cardmargin}
\setlength{\cardmargin}{0pt}% default => two side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<

\setlength{\cardwidthspace}{18pt} % add right horizontal space
\setlength{\cardheightspace}{20pt}% add upper vertical space

% \setlength{\cardmargin}{\cardwidthspace}  % use for one side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<           

\usepackage{etoolbox}   % for the patch 
\patchcmd{\card}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)\advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax\advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax}
{}{}

\patchcmd{\card}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)%
        \advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax%
        \advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax%
        \advance\@tempdimb by \cardmargin\relax% 
    }
{}{}

\renewcommand{\cardtextstylef}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}
\renewcommand{\cardtextstyleb}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}

\newcommand{\flashcard}[1]{% create new command for cards with blanks
    \card{% call the original \card command with twice the same argument (#1)
        \let\blank\frontcard% but let \blank behave like \frontcard the first time
        #1
    }{%
        \let\blank\backcard% and like \backcard the second time
        #1
    }%
}

%% Set front head & back foot for dfs
\renewcommand{\flhead}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | Verb}}
\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | Verb }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{vera} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Það \textcolor{red}{\underline{er}} mín afstaða í þessu máli. }} 
{vera \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[vɛːra]} \\
en.: \emph{be; stay} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & er -- var -- verið \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & ert -- varst -- verið \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & er -- var -- verið \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

{af \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{prep.})}} \\[1ex]

af (Indeclinable)}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | Noun }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{grein} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{f.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hann skrifar langa \textcolor{red}{\underline{grein}} í miðopnu Morgunblaðsins í dag. }}
{grein \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{f.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[kreiːn]} \\
en.: \emph{branch; subject, field; article} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) grein -- (til) greinar \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) greinum -- (til) greina \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{stór} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Þetta er \textcolor{red}{\underline{stór}} dagur. }}
{stór \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[stouːr]} \\
en.: \emph{large; tall} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & stór  --  stór -- stórt \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & stærri -- stærri -- stærra \\ 
\textsc{superl}: & stærstur -- stærst -- stærst \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{langur} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Veður var afar slæmt og tóku björgunaraðgerðir \textcolor{red}{\underline{langan}} tíma fyrir vikið. }}
{langur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[lauŋkʏr]} \\
en.: \emph{long} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & langur  --  löng -- langt \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & lengri -- lengri -- lengra \\ 
\textsc{superl}: & lengstur -- lengst -- lengst \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{heimur} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Talið er að þessi dómur geti haft áhrif um allan \textcolor{red}{\underline{heim}} . }}
{heimur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[heiːmʏr]} \\
en.: \emph{world} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) heimi -- (til) heims \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) heimum -- (til) heima \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{stefna} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{ \textcolor{red}{\underline{Stefnt}} er að því söluferlið taki stuttan tíma. }} 
{stefna \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[stɛpna]} \\
en.: \emph{head; strive for; indict} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & stefni -- stefndi -- stefnt \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & stefnir -- stefndir -- stefnt \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & stefnir -- stefndi -- stefnt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | Noun }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{hlutverk} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hækkun íbúðaverðs spilar þar stórt \textcolor{red}{\underline{hlutverk}} . }}
{hlutverk \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[l̥ʏːtvɛr̥k]} \\
en.: \emph{role; part} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) hlutverki -- (til) hlutverks \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) hlutverkum -- (til) hlutverka \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | Verb }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{skipa} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Búið er að \textcolor{red}{\underline{skipa}} formenn allra fastanefnda Alþingis. }} 
{skipa \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[scɪːpa]} \\
en.: \emph{command; appoint; occupy} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & skipa -- skipaði -- skipað \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & skipar -- skipaðir -- skipað \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & skipar -- skipaði -- skipað \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

{Telst nú í reynd \textcolor{red}{\underline{auðveldara}} að fá örorkumat en áður. }}
{auðveldur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[œiðvɛltʏr]} \\
en.: \emph{easy, simple} \\  [2ex]

\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & auðveldur  --  auðveld -- auðvelt \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & auðveldari -- auðveldari -- auðveldara \\ 
\textsc{superl}: & auðveldastur -- auðveldust -- auðveldast \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{ \textcolor{red}{\underline{Norska}} ríkisútvarpið greindi frá þessu fyrir stundu. }}
{norskur \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[nɔr̥skʏr]} \\
en.: \emph{Norwegian} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & norskur  --  norsk -- norskt \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & norskari -- norskari -- norskara \\ 
\textsc{superl}: & norskastur -- norskust -- norskast \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | Noun }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{samtök} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\ [2ex]
{ \textcolor{red}{\underline{Samtökin}} eru ósátt við hvalveiðar Íslendinga. }}
{samtök \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[samtʰœk]} \\
en.: \emph{association, union} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá)  -- (til)  \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) samtökum -- (til) samtaka \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{Almenningi er gefinn kostur á að \textcolor{red}{\underline{móta}} verkefni. }} 
{móta \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[mouːta]} \\
en.: \emph{form, shape; model} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & móta -- mótaði -- mótað \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & mótar -- mótaðir -- mótað \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & mótar -- mótaði -- mótað \\ 
\end{tabular}
}
